6/30/25:
	-Back in Sasserine, the whole crew and I headed straight to a bar.
		-I got the first round, and got the party started!
		-Gradually, some of the party snuck off to attend to various bits of business, but us
		 hardcore party people kept at it.
		-Soon I was buying whiskey-and-oil cocktails for an animated chain named Frank that had
		 slithered down from upstairs, trying to set it up with my boots, and dancing on a table.
		-Grimble set up a small alchemist lab on a nearby table and got to brewing something firey,
		 though he had to keep slapping away the hands of crew members that tried to grab and drink
		 from the beakers.


8/11/25:
	-A month, and many drinks later. . .
	-Maybe _too_ many drinks. . . as I heard some clinking and, looking down, there was a
     surprisingly well dressed chicken pecking at my glass of whiskey.
		-Naturally, I offered to buy the chicken a drink of his own. . . but got about the response
		 you'd expect from a chicken, with him cocking his head and looking at me quizzically.
		-About that time a(nother) gnome, dressed in wizard robes, burst into the bar, yelling,
		 "Grab that chicken!"
		-I shrugged and made a grab for the bird, but only caught a feather as the chicken
		 _teleported_ across the room.
		-Several of my crewmates seemed to be game for the chase too, with D'Roc trying the seize
		 the bird also, but crashing into furniture instead, and Lucien trying to scare the bird
		 into submission (turns out terrified chickens don't hold still).
		-After a few moments, the chicken started making for the open door.
		-Pretty though I may be, I decided to try using my head. . . and hypnotized the chicken.
		-D'Roc took the opportunity to take hold of the chicken.
		-"So, the bird's not going anywhere for a bit," I began, addressing the new gnome. "What's
		  this all about?"
		 "That bird owes me a drink!" the gnome replied. "Out of a very special goblet, in fact. . ."
		-He went on to explain that the chicken had somehow stolen this goblet from him, and hidden
		 it from him.
			-"Of course, he wasn't always a chicken. . . A spell rebounded, there was a magic
			  accident, you know how it goes."
		-"Well. . . How do your propose to interrogate this chicken?" I asked the gnome.
		 "I'd been planning to detect his thoughts. . . though I'm not sure that's an option, while
		  you are. . . doing. . . whatever you've done here."
		 "Ah! Well, D'Roc, got a good hold on him?"
		 "Wait!" the gnome interjected. "Hang on. Let me cast something first, to anchor him here.
		  Don't want him teleporting off again. . ."
		 "Oh! Yeah, prudent!"
		-The gnome went about muttering some arcane symbols and such, and then nodded to me when the
		 spell was complete.
		-I released my hold on the chicken's mind and he began to struggle in D'Roc's grasp but
		 couldn't get free.
		-"Thank you very much for your help," the gnome said. "What's the fee for chicken catching
		  these days? Here, have a hundred gold. . . I'll take the chicken, then, and be on my way."
		-That seemed a surprising but welcome sum to me. . . but Bruce raised a hand. Walking over
		 to me, he whispered, "Keep the gnome talking. Something is suspicious. . ." He then went
		 over to confer with Jade.
		-I began pestering the gnome about the best liquors to fill a fancy goblet and such while
		 Jade fiddled with a stick she'd pulled out from her pack, applying various substances to
		 it while muttering.
		-The gnome seemed eager to get out of there but D'Roc wasn't handing over the chicken.
		-After a few moments, Jade took her stick and bonked the chicken on his head. . . and the
		 chicken proceeded to turn into a naked man clutching tiny chicken clothes to his loins.
			-"Wait," I demanded. "The clothes didn't change with him?!? Someone is making tiny
			  chicken finery! What have we gotten involved in?!?"
			-Jade grabbed him a tea towel from the bar.
		-At this point, D'Roc noticed the strange gnome beginning to sidle towards the door, and
		 shouted to Lucien, who stood near the gnome, to grab him.
		-In the blink of an eye, Lucien had one hand on the gnome and another on a knife at the
		 little guy's throat.
		-Talking to the mostly-nude former-chicken, we quickly learned that:
			-He was a young noble of House Lorchester, minor nobility of Sasserine.
			-This gnome was part of a group that ambushed him one night as he was walking home
			 drunk, turning him into a chicken and kidnapping him, presumably for ransom.
		-He asked if we would walk him back to his family, who would surely offer a reward.
			-Maya asked that the Lorchester grant us a commensurate favor, instead of cash, and he
		     eagerly agreed.
			-Jade pointed out we should find him some clothes first, and Maya chimed in asking
			 Grimble if his theater troupe kin were still in Sasserine, they having provided us
			 tailoring in the past.
				-He nodded and fluttered out the door in search of them.
				-A drink or two later, he returned with a rather garish noble costume, something
				 suited to a play.
				-After young Lorchester got dressed, D'Roc whispered to me and pointed out that
				 there were subtle chickens sewed and embroidered into various bits of the garments.
					-_So_ glad to have you back, Grimble!
	-We then escorted the young nobleman back to his family's estate.
		-They were not _quite_ thrilled to see him, in a way that painted him as something of an
		 embarassment, and casting some amount of doubt on the value of the favor he'll be able to
		 wring from his kin.
	-Afterwards, we took some time to interrogate our gnomish chicken knapper.
		-Maya was particularly offended that they were preying on the nobles of _her_ city.
			-And, I suspect, saw some political advancement for her to be seen stopping it.
		-He was easily intimidated, but also clearly not the mastermind of this all, nor powerful
		 enough a wizard to have accomplished the polymorph.
		-He said he was part of a gang led by a halfling with long red hair that sticks straight
		 up and a distinctive scar.
		-He also admitted they were planning to kidnap another noble after an upcoming feast, in
		 three days time.
			-That event turned out to by _Maya's_ party.
			-Now it's _personal_.
			-"Also, Maya. . . I wasn't invited?!?" I asked, incredulous.
			 "But I _did_ invite you, Fred!" she replied. ". . . you must have forgotten, in your
			  time at that bar."
			 "Oh. That sounds likely."
		-With Jade's help, and the perfidious gnome's description, we employed scrying magic to see
		 the image of our halfling mastermind.
			-He indeed looked like the kind of creepy fuck that would be turning people into
			 chickens. . . and sewing tiny outfits for them: https://discord.com/channels/560915739796570113/560915739796570119/1404652962231488582
			-He sat at table writing letters, surrounded by animals. . . also in tiny noble
			 outfits?!? It was like some kind of demented petting zoo.
			-Bruce, peering closely into the mirror Jade had worked her scrying magic with, was
			 able to identify the letters as _invoices_, not ransom notes as we'd presumed, which
			 fortunately included an address on Cloud street.


8/26/25:
	-(I missed a session due to the broken toe.)


9/22/25:
	-Well, everyone seemed quite keen to follow up on all sorts of leads but, after a month's binge
	 drinking. . . I really needed a drink. So, I volunteered to watch the prisoner.
		-I didn't have any shackles or the like, but. . . "Hey, you're pint-sized. . ." I said to
		 the gnome. "How many pints can you hold?"
		 "A surprising amount," he claimed, so we went back to the bar to test that.
			-I figured he can't run off if he can't walk, let alone in a straight line.
		-Back at the bar, we went straight to shots. I matched him one for one, but soon caught him
		 trying to cheat by spilling liquor on the floor.
		-"Oh!" I exclaimed. "My shoes should get in on this!"
		-Looking down at my boots, I said, "Jaspar! If I pour some rum down you, you're not going
		 to go teleporting it away into some nearby chamber pot or. . . _gnome_. . . again, are you?"
		-Jaspar took my meaning and, after a long pour of rum, our prisoner couldn't even _sit_
		 upright.
		-Though the gnome could now barely speak, he _did_ seem to be trying to cast some kind of
		 spell, mumbling requests for various components.
			-I just kept handing him various things I found around the bar: pickled eggs, old corks,
			 and the like. Needless to say, he didn't get very far.
	-Eventually the party came to find me.
		-They were all talking over each other, telling me about someone planning to build some kind
		 spider-flesh golem, digging up bits from the pits around the arena (given all it's fantastic
		 beast combats and such).
			-I didn't quite catch how this was connected to the kidnapping, but, well, they were
			 excited by the matter and I figured, eh, what the hells.
		-After some discussion of how we could track these nefarious spider stitchers down, Maya
		 threw out the idea of luring them to _us_.
			-From what they'd learned and what Jade knew of the construct construction process, they
			 had plenty of _parts_, but needed a soul to animate the thing.
			-Maya proposed spreading a rumor about the discovery of some trapped and especially
			 desirable soul, like that of a half-god, and I took the idea and ran with it.
				-We had a quick discussion of where we'd try to lure these freaks _to_ and, after
				 Jade seemed none too excited by Maya's proposal of her magic shop, we settled on
				 the old temple in that cavern on a nearby isle where the Shapers had been making
				 their weresharks.
			-I spent the rest of the evening popping into half the taverns in the city, talking
			 about how some remnants of the Shapers had found a crystal containing the soul of a
			 child of Lolth, _the_ thing you'd want for any spider-abominations you'd happen to be
			 building, and that they had stashed the thing at their old temple.
				-Word spread like wildfire, probably because I'm so amazing at everything, and,
				 before we'd turned in for the night, the city was buzzing with the rumor.
				-We even saw vendors selling bracelets and charms featuring sharks with spider legs!
				 They work fast!
	-Arriving the temple-cavern, it was much as we left it: drenched in blood. . . but the _corpses_
	 were gone. . .
		-Well, that being a bit suspicious, D'Roc and Maya went to go search the place for evidence
		 of what happened to the bodies while the rest of us began getting stuff set up.
		-The first sign something was wrong Maya beginning to say, "D'Roc. . ."
		-That was followed by a thud and and thunderous "Ugh!" of disgust from our might minotaur.
		-Looking in their direction, I saw D'Roc being accosted by an animate mass of disgusting
		 black ooze.
		-. . . I wisely ran for some cover, in the opposite direction.
		-Maya blasted the ooze, though, to it's seeming dismay, and D'Roc, with somewhat more. . .
		 complicated effect, cleaved the ooze in twain. . . only for both halves of the mass to
		 continue lunging at him with disgusting psuedopods.
		-Grimble, laughing, pointed out the stuff looked like pitch and, fluttering into the air for
		 a good vantage point, blasted both halves with a gout of fire, setting them aflame.
		-Things rapidly devolved into chaos, with the ooze getting split futher, one blob swallowing
		 D'Roc for a bit, and, tragically, one blob swatting Maya's very brave little pet dragon out
		 of the air, where it fell limply into a stream of water.
		-Fortunately D'Roc managed to very messily burst out of the filthy thing, though he looked
		 pretty badly worse for the wear.
		-Also delightfully, Jade managed to fish the tiny dragon from the water and Bruce ran over
		 to minister to the critter's wounds.
		-After that, D'Roc wisely stood back, hurling handy boulders at the things instead, while
		 Maya and Grimble more metaphorically hurled eldritch energies their way, and soon the ooze
		 was. . . well, at least no longer mobile.
	-After that, we saw to setting up our ambush.
		-Maya and I spent some time getting her made up to look like a _very_ convincing drow,
		 figuring that might come in handy.
		-I then identified some useful fighting positions while Jade and D'Roc began setting up
		 various traps.
